.. index:: pair: function; snd_config_substitute
.. _doxid-conf_8c_1a0c4acd2de7999ad6e477d398662485c2:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	snd_config_substitute(
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* dst,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* src
	)

Substitutes one configuration node to another.

If both nodes are compounds, the source compound node members are appended to the destination compound node.

If the destination node is a compound and the source node is an ordinary type, the compound members are deleted (including their contents).

Otherwise, the source node's value replaces the destination node's value.

In any case, a successful call to this function frees the source node.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- dst

		- Handle to the destination node.

	*
		- src

		- Handle to the source node. Must not be the same as *dst*.



.. rubric:: Returns:

Zero if successful, otherwise a negative error code.

	snd_config_get_type_ascii(

		- 

	*

		- 

	*
		- real<dt>::SND_CONFIG_TYPE_REAL

		- 

	*
		- string<dt>::SND_CONFIG_TYPE_STRING

		- 

	*
		- compound<dt>::SND_CONFIG_TYPE_COMPOUND

		-

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- -EINVAL

		- Unknown note type in *type*.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::

		- ascii

		- A string containing a configuration node type.

	*
		- type

		- The node type corresponding to *ascii*.



.. rubric:: Returns:

Zero if successful, otherwise a negative error code.

.. index:: pair: function; snd_config_remove
.. _doxid-conf_8c_1ad4d69b003662e09e8206a7892e849d27:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	snd_config_remove(:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* config)

Removes a configuration node from its tree.

This function makes *config* a top-level node, i.e., if *config* has a parent, then *config* is removed from the list of the parent's children.

This functions does *not* free the removed node.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- config

		- Handle to the configuration node to be removed.



.. rubric:: Returns:

Zero if successful, otherwise a negative error code.



.. rubric:: See also:

:ref:`snd_config_delete <doxid-group___config_1ga2a006b942faa3335a958a7df7bcea17e>`

.. index:: pair: function; snd_config_searcha
.. _doxid-conf_8c_1af0f5cf4dde9399e3aadc53b4ab1d5059:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	snd_config_searcha(
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* root,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* config,
		const char* key,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`** result
	)

Searches for a node in a configuration tree, expanding aliases.

This functions searches for a child node of *config* like :ref:`snd_config_search <doxid-group___config_1gabafb8cac2181c4c1e34b99f54421d1c6>`. However, any compound node can also be identified by an alias, which is a string node whose value is taken as the id of a compound node below *root*.

*root* must be a compound node. *root* and *config* may be the same node.

For example, with the following configuration, the call

.. ref-code-block:: cpp

	snd_config_searcha(root, config, "a.b.c.d", &result);

would return the node with id ``d:``

.. ref-code-block:: cpp

	config {
	    a {
	        b bb
	    }
	}
	root {
	    bb {
	        c cc
	    }
	    cc ccc
	    ccc {
	        d {
	            x "icks"
	        }
	    }
	}

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- -ENOENT

		- An id in *key* or an alias id does not exist.

	*
		- -ENOENT

		- *config* or one of its child nodes to be searched is not a compound or string node.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- root

		- Handle to the root configuration node containing alias definitions.

	*
		- config

		- Handle to the root of the configuration (sub)tree to search.

	*
		- key

		- Search key: one or more node keys, separated with dots.

	*
		- result

		- When *result*!= ``NULL``, the function puts the handle to the node found at the address specified by *result*.



.. rubric:: Returns:

Zero if successful, otherwise a negative error code.

.. index:: pair: function; snd_config_searchva
.. _doxid-conf_8c_1a11646339b1555e9a36a3da3327a0bd6a:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	snd_config_searchva(
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* root,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* config,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`** result,
		...
	)

Searches for a node in a configuration tree, expanding aliases.

This function searches for a child node of *config*, allowing aliases, like :ref:`snd_config_searcha <doxid-conf_8c_1af0f5cf4dde9399e3aadc53b4ab1d5059>`, but the search key is the concatenation of all passed seach key strings, like with :ref:`snd_config_searchv <doxid-group___config_1ga7b2f5723e44a1b69f2a8555d469803d1>`.

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- -ENOENT

		- An id in a search key does not exist.

	*
		- -ENOENT

		- *config* or one of its child nodes to be searched is not a compound or string node.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- root

		- Handle to the root configuration node containing alias definitions.

	*
		- config

		- Handle to the root of the configuration (sub)tree to search.

	*
		- result

		- When *result*!= ``NULL``, the function puts the handle to the node found at the address specified by *result*.

	*
		- ...

		- One or more concatenated dot separated search keys, terminated with ``NULL``.



.. rubric:: Returns:

Zero if successful, otherwise a negative error code.

.. index:: pair: function; snd_config_search_alias
.. _doxid-conf_8c_1a95836105fb9cdb3ff6fb674d3a297fdb:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	snd_config_search_alias(
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* config,
		const char* base,
		const char* key,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`** result
	)

Searches for a node in a configuration tree, expanding aliases.

This functions searches for a child node of *config*, allowing aliases, like :ref:`snd_config_searcha <doxid-conf_8c_1af0f5cf4dde9399e3aadc53b4ab1d5059>`. However, alias definitions are searched below *config* (there is no separate *root* parameter), and *base* specifies a seach key that identifies a compound node that is used to search for an alias definitions that is not found directly below *config* and that does not contain a period. In other words, when ``"id"`` is not found in *config*, this function also tries ``"base.id"``.

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- -ENOENT

		- An id in *key* or an alias id does not exist.

	*
		- -ENOENT

		- *config* or one of its child nodes to be searched is not a compound or string node.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- config

		- Handle to the root of the configuration (sub)tree to search.

	*
		- base

		- Search key base, or ``NULL``.

	*
		- key

		- Search key suffix.

	*
		- result

		- When *result*!= ``NULL``, the function puts the handle to the node found at the address specified by *result*.



.. rubric:: Returns:

Zero if successful, otherwise a negative error code.

.. index:: pair: function; snd_config_search_hooks
.. _doxid-conf_8c_1ad6a8a7b3b67b8f755ab60073bec5fd48:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	snd_config_search_hooks(
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* config,
		const char* key,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`** result
	)

Searches for a node in a configuration tree and expands hooks.

This functions searches for a child node of *config* like :ref:`snd_config_search <doxid-group___config_1gabafb8cac2181c4c1e34b99f54421d1c6>`, but any compound nodes to be searched that contain hooks are modified by the respective hook functions.

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- -ENOENT

		- An id in *key* does not exist.

	*
		- -ENOENT

		- *config* or one of its child nodes to be searched is not a compound node.

Additionally, any errors encountered when parsing the hook definitions or returned by the hook functions.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- config

		- Handle to the root of the configuration (sub)tree to search.

	*
		- key

		- Search key: one or more node keys, separated with dots.

	*
		- result

		- The function puts the handle to the node found at the address specified by *result*.



.. rubric:: Returns:

Zero if successful, otherwise a negative error code.

.. index:: pair: function; snd_config_hook_load_for_all_cards
.. _doxid-conf_8c_1ac64a8c73293ee35ed3f3958d47bdc721:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	snd_config_hook_load_for_all_cards(
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* root,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* config,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`** dst,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* private_data
	)

Loads and parses the given configurations files for each installed sound card.

This function works like :ref:`snd_config_hook_load <doxid-conf_8c_1a4008d77ad63047366463350b7726a5ec>`, but the files are loaded once for each sound card. The driver name is available with the ``private_string`` function to customize the file name.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- root

		- Handle to the root configuration node.

	*
		- config

		- Handle to the configuration node for this hook.

	*
		- dst

		- The function puts the handle to the configuration node loaded from the file(s) at the address specified by *dst*.

	*
		- private_data

		- Handle to the private data configuration node.



.. rubric:: Returns:

Zero if successful, otherwise a negative error code.

.. index:: pair: function; snd_func_getenv
.. _doxid-confmisc_8c_1a033eab97ee6619aeb8c5eca585acf6c0:

	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	snd_func_getenv(
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`** dst,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* root,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* src,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* private_data
	)

Returns an environment value.

Example:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp

	{
	    @func getenv
	    vars [ MY_CARD CARD C ]
	    default 0
	}



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- dst

		- The function puts the handle to the result configuration node (with type string) at the address specified by ``dst``.

	*
		- root

		- Handle to the root source node.

	*
		- src

		- Handle to the source node, with definitions for ``vars`` and ``default``.

	*
		- private_data

		- Handle to the ``private_data`` node.



.. rubric:: Returns:

Zero if successful, otherwise a negative error code.

.. index:: pair: function; snd_func_refer
.. _doxid-confmisc_8c_1a8d91af8387a708c526bac3ee2c7ea10e:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	snd_func_refer(
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`** dst,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* root,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* src,
		:ref:`snd_config_t<doxid-group___config_1ga1c20905af775ae77d04d1a5696f67985>`* private_data
	)

Copies the specified configuration node.

.. note::

	The root source node can be modified!

Example:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp

	{
	    @func refer
	    file "/etc/myconf.conf"     # optional
	    name "id1.id2.id3"
	}



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- dst

		- The function puts the handle to the result configuration node (with the same type as the specified node) at the address specified by ``dst``.

	*
		- root

		- Handle to the root source node.

	*
		- src

		- Handle to the source node, with definitions for ``name`` and (optionally) ``file``.

	*
		- private_data

		- Handle to the ``private_data`` node.



.. rubric:: Returns:

A non-negative value if successful, otherwise a negative error code.

.. index:: pair: function; snd_lib_error_default
.. _doxid-error_8c_1aca34eed0a74b5d51332e62b568483d4f:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	static
	void
	snd_lib_error_default(
		const char* file,
		int line,
		const char* function,
		int err,
		const char* fmt,
		...
	)

The default error handler function.

If a local error function has been installed for the current thread by :ref:`snd_lib_error_set_local <doxid-error_8c_1a88c091aae3b291d5097078dd39f42408>`, it is called. Otherwise, prints the error message including location to ``stderr``.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- file

		- The filename where the error was hit.

	*
		- line

		- The line number.

	*
		- function

		- The function name.

	*
		- err

		- The error code.

	*
		- fmt

		- The message (including the format characters).

	*
		- ...

		- Optional arguments.

.. _doxid-pcm__file_8c_1a2d295a1bebec45e0541de03b86de0703:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	snd_pcm_file_open(
		:ref:`snd_pcm_t<doxid-group___p_c_m_1ga919e634deecd855b6e2e15174e70d3ea>`** pcmp,
		const char* name,
		const char* fname,
		int fd,
		const char* ifname,
		int ifd,
		int trunc,
		const char* fmt,
		int perm,
		:ref:`snd_pcm_t<doxid-group___p_c_m_1ga919e634deecd855b6e2e15174e70d3ea>`* slave,
		int close_slave,
		:ref:`snd_pcm_stream_t<doxid-group___p_c_m_1gac23b43ff55add78638e503b9cc892c24>` stream
	)

Creates a new File PCM.

.. warning::

	Using of this function might be dangerous in the sense of compatibility reasons. The prototype might be freely changed in future.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- pcmp

		- Returns created PCM handle

	*
		- name

		- Name of PCM

	*
		- fname

		- Output filename (or NULL if file descriptor fd is available)

	*
		- fd

		- Output file descriptor

	*
		- ifname

		- Input filename (or NULL if file descriptor ifd is available)

	*
		- ifd

		- Input file descriptor (if (ifd < 0) && (ifname == NULL), no input redirection will be performed)

	*
		- trunc

		- Truncate the file if it already exists

	*
		- fmt

		- File format ("raw" or "wav" are available)

	*
		- perm

		- File permission

	*
		- slave

		- Slave PCM handle

	*
		- close_slave

		- When set, the slave PCM handle is closed with copy PCM

	*
		- stream

		- the direction of PCM stream

	*
		- zero

		- on success otherwise a negative error code

	*

	*

		- Slave PCM handle

	*
		- close_slave

	*
		- zero

		- on success otherwise a negative error code
